 Empire: C:\cevict-live\apps\progno >

 Empire: C:\cevict-live\apps\progno > # Clear output file if exists

 Empire: C:\cevict-live\apps\progno > if (Test-Path $OutputFile) { Remove-Item $OutputFile -Force }

 Empire: C:\cevict-live\apps\progno >

 Empire: C:\cevict-live\apps\progno > Write-Output "Exporting key PROGNO files for Grok..." | Out-File -FilePath $OutputFile -Encoding utf8

 Empire: C:\cevict-live\apps\progno >

 Empire: C:\cevict-live\apps\progno > foreach ($file in $FilesToExport) {
>>     if (Test-Path $file) {
>>         Write-Output "`n`n=== FILENAME: $file ===" | Out-File -FilePath $OutputFile -Append -Encoding utf8
>>         Write-Output "=== START CONTENT ===" | Out-File -FilePath $OutputFile -Append -Encoding utf8
>>         Get-Content $file -Raw | Out-File -FilePath $OutputFile -Append -Encoding utf8
>>         Write-Output "`n=== END CONTENT ===" | Out-File -FilePath $OutputFile -Append -Encoding utf8
>>     } else {
>>         # Try common alternative paths
>>         $altPaths = @(
>>             "app/$file",
>>             "components/$file",
>>             "lib/$file",
>>             "src/app/$file",
>>             "src/components/$file",
>>             "src/lib/$file"
>>         )
>>         $found = $false
>>         foreach ($alt in $altPaths) {
>>             if (Test-Path $alt) {
>>                 Write-Output "`n`n=== FILENAME (found alt): $alt ===" | Out-File -FilePath $OutputFile -Append -Encoding utf8
>>                 Write-Output "=== START CONTENT ===" | Out-File -FilePath $OutputFile -Append -Encoding utf8
>>                 Get-Content $alt -Raw | Out-File -FilePath $OutputFile -Append -Encoding utf8
>>                 Write-Output "`n=== END CONTENT ===" | Out-File -FilePath $OutputFile -Append -Encoding utf8
>>                 $found = $true
>>                 break
>>             }
>>         }
>>         if (-not $found) {
>>             Write-Output "`n`n=== FILE NOT FOUND: $file (and alternatives) ===" | Out-File -FilePath $OutputFile -Append -Encoding utf8
>>         }
>>     }
>> }
